< Review>
Incredibly beautiful, and the acoustics were spectacular. We went on the opening weekend and the food service was a bit disorganised, but it tasted good and you can beat the location! If you have a wheelchair I recommend calling the box office to reserve your tickets. There was some confusion with handicapped seating because the online seat map did not match some of the actual wheelchair/companion seating.</Review>

< review>
The three stars I am offering up are mainly for the construction crews who did a fantastic job throughout the project. These guys kicked hiney and I spent enough time very near their location to see them actually building this structure for several months. Diligent and professional as they could be and friendly as passer-byes with their inquisiting minds passed by. I'm looking forward to returning here to see something in person.

When they were installed the lighting system I remember thinking as I looked in that direction it seemed as if the sun rose and set in succession again and again at night as they programmed it to function like it was supposed to.  It was
very neat to see something like that coming to life.

My best wishes for this venue and it's upcoming events!  During this time or I should say phase of our health consciousness, it will do good to see something bring happiness and joy to those who visit and not to mention it's fantastic location on the bay.

~JR~</review>

< text>
Everybody at Scripps West Dental is the best.  I've been a patient for maybe over 10+ years and I always feel like family every time I visit.  Dr. Tasto is my dentist and he is very friendly. He thoroughly explains what's going on with my teeth. Monica is my hygienist. She is really good at what she does.  She listens to my concerns and she addresses them if she can, or she provides advice what I should do to prevent it get worst. She then explains it to Dr. Tasto so he can evaluate it.  She is the one who inspired me to floss my teeth every day, which really helped to keep my teeth healthy.  The staffs in front office are friendlier as ever.  I highly recommend this dental clinic..< /text>

<name>Kim Cochran<//name><time>1420960373762</time><Rating>5</Rating><Review>Gave Dickey’s one more try after a few people told us it had a new owner and turned around. WOW - Really impressed today!

First time, just after the business opened, they were out of brisket and all chicken, tried again cause they were local. Second time we waited 20 mins to be served (NOBODY ELSE IN THE RESTAURANT) so we walked out.

Today Dickey’s, its new owner Alex, and their staff, redeemed themselves 10 fold. We were welcomed when we entered the store which was not only clean but busy! The few empty tables were clean and ready for occupancy. I crossed my fingers and ordered the 2 item plate with both brisket and pulled pork. I chose the green beans and mashed potato casserole for my sides. The meal also included a roll which was nice and fresh. The meat was hot, plentiful and flavorful. Just the right amount of smoke flavor. The sides were served hot and tasted great.

There were 3 in my party so I had the opportunity to try the turkey sandwich, onion strings, coleslaw, mac and cheese and ribs as well. Not one bad item in the entire order! Really great to finally have a local bbq place I can count on to satisfy my cravings and know it will be great!< /Review>< Pics>

one covered with delicious thick green-tea infused whipped cream individually and then all stacked together. Now imagine.. on top of this there is a matcha powder of the finest quality getting dusted... surreal isnt it? I tasted this surreal-ness just about last weekend!! I saw Lady M store during my visit to NY 2 weeks ago. I looked it up on yelp and I sooo wanted to try it but unfortunately, it was closed. When I came back to the bay, randomly searched again (good for me!!) and guess what, saw a ladyM popup at Los Altos!

First thing first, their staff is great and ofcourse mille crepes are unbeatable! And the teas...aahhh..so light and perfectly balanced with flavors.
I'd give them a 4/5 for pricing but honestly I won't be too bothered about it, you truly get your money's worth.
The menu is pretty elaborate and have good choices of items. They seem to make everything from scratch each day. You can either get a slice or can even order a cake.
They also had a little display for Royce Chocolates. I took the Champagne and matcha one for home and also their potato chips dipped in chocolate! Believe me: you would definitely want to grab the chips! You'll go bonkers with the play of taste!

Here's the items I tried and my recommendations:

1. Classic Mille Crepe: Do not MISS this one!! I repeat: DO NOT MISS THIS ONE. Have  it and you will thank me for life! The crepe were so well done and merged together with the cream in such harmony, you wouldn't even realize the crepes are even there! I think this is the exact item I would go again for lifetime now. Also, needless to say, it was 5/5.

2. Matcha Green Tea Mille Crepe: I am not high on matcha and green tea but this was their staff recommended item and honestly I was not disappointed. There is something so elite and grande about this slice, you can feel that every item that goes into making it is of a supreme quality and has been freshly made.

3. Berry Mont Blanc Tart: Sweet cream with a hint of sour, perfect dessert for after dinner for me! I'd love to grab this for after dinner and have it with some green tea or chai. The base was of a good consistency, not too hard and neither too soft to mess up the taste. Good amount of flavor, I tasted hints of rose which was great! For me this was a definite 5/5.

4. Teas: Rose tea and Matcha Green Tea: I liked them. They did not feel too milky and thankfully the taste of the flavor did not overpower the overall tea taste. I'd recommend trying them without the desserts on the side. Everything gets too sweet and kind of spoils the experience.

Lastly, they are going to make the pop-up a permanent location for Lady M! Yaaaay!<//Review><gmapID>0x808fb1b26237fb57:0xd281eb0dd4492a4a<//gmapID></record></dataset><record>

< review>
Lady M is apparently the gold standard in mille crepes in the bay area and although I can't compare it to any other, it's quite a delight. For the uninitiated, a mille crepes is essentially about twenty to twenty five layers of crepes with cream in between them. Yes, it does actually taste as good as it sounds.

Lady M call's itself a cake boutique and that is exactly how it feels like walking into the store. The decor is very classy and chic with a lot of white with subtle highlights.

There is not a great deal of choice with about six to eight flavors on offer at any point. We tried the signature, green tea, chocolate and tiramisu flavors which were pretty good. The signature was definitely the pick of the lot and the green tea was very interesting. The crepes themselves were nice and soft, easily able to be cut with a fork. The cream was perfectly light and sweet. The slices are definitely on the smaller side and at about $9 a slice, they definitely feel like a splurge. Although they specialize in crepe cakes, they do have a couple flavors of regular cakes as well.

Crepe cakes feel like the fancy cousin of regular cakes and Lady M definitely does a great job at them. Definitely worth going back for that signature slice!< /review>

<name>Amir Ahmed Asif<//name><date>1579516198763</date>< rate>

< review>
It is famous for a reason! If you have a chance, please try a cake 🍰 here. This super-thin crepe layers separated by creme -is something that everyone should try. We had Green Tea and Pistachio Mille Crepe Cakes. And, I am happy to say, the hype is well deserved. The thin crepe layers break the monotonous "cake-cream-cake" tradition. The layers are very well balanced. The cream's sweetness is just at the 'sweet spot'. I liked the green tea one more than the pistachio (and it is the other way for my wife: she liked her pistachio).
We arrived just 10 minutes before open, and was second in line. At the opening time, people were forming lines at the door. Once opened, the lines move fairly quick, and the there are some sitting arrangements inside for dine-in. The interior is simple and clean (it is a pop up).
They also have coffee and it is nice to grab a cup with a cake.
Overall, Lady M 'takes the Cake' (pun intended).< /review>

The first day they open after the New Year holiday (closed Jan 1 to Jan 9).
It is a Friday. They open at 10am, I came 10:05am, there are already 30-40 people in line. 99% of the people are ordering for to go.

Waited about 30min until my turn to order. I got the seasonal Earl Gray Mille Crepe cake. 9 inch for $95 ($90 for same size original or green tea). After I ordered mine, I heard the stuffs saying no more Earl Gray.

Parking
Their is a small parking lot, but parking may be an issue if you go during peak time.

They don't have phone number or other type of contact for preorder.</text>

The location is good and the interior is the feeling of Lady M. Originally it was a popup, but it is said to be changed to a permanent. It is said to be decorated like a flagship store. The signature cake is fresher than anything in Korea. The espresso machine also has faith in Lamarzzo. The beans are lightly roasted and feel soft. Uniquely located is the Japanese Royce Chocolate Display Stand. More expensive than Japan.

<review>I give this company 3 out of 5 stars

Pros: The website was one of the more professional looking sites. The crew that hauled out my junk were great guys (positive, professional and quick).

Cons: My experience was not ideal. I reached out on Saturday looking for junk removal and they scheduled me for Sunday between 2:30pm - 3:30pm. The weather said it was going to rain Sunday and I asked them if it was going to be an issue and they said no. I received a call at 3:33pm letting me know they were going to be late by 1.5 to 2 hours due to being held up with another job. I said that was fine. I then received another call at 5pm saying the dump had closed due to rain (something I would have thought they knew might happen - doubt this was the very first time the dump closed due to rain). They rescheduled me for Monday and originally gave me a $10 discount for a job they were charging $399 for. I was annoyed by the low ball discount but the manager texted me a little later and acknowledged that the $10 discount was inadequate. He changed it to a 10% discount ($39) which I thought was much more reasonable. The service would now be $360.

Here is where things went south again. When the haulers arrived Monday, they told me the futon mattress I needed them to take was going to cost an extra $60. This seemed ridiculous to me since I said I needed a mattress removed in my original request. If they missed that in the original communications, that’s on them. It should have been part of the original quote (I have the text message that says “futon frame and mattress”). They also told me the room was larger then they thought so it would cost more. After the haulers talked to their boss, they said it was going to cost $460 WITH THE 10% discount. This is $100 more then what I was told after having to be rescheduled. I told the haulers to just leave the mattress (which is still here) and take everything else. I told them I only had $425 in cash (I told the owner I was paying in cash in the original communications - springing extra charges on last minute is super inconvenient when a customer is paying in cash) and that’s all I could pay. The haulers accepted it and completed the job.

Do I feel like this was a little bit of a bait and switch? Yeah. Do I feel like the owner should have done a better job getting info for the estimate? Yeah. Could he have easily asked for a list of items in the room that were (for example) over 25lbs; bigger than a breadbox; etc? Yeah. Could he have asked for more pics, video that scanned the room, measurements for the room to give a more accurate estimate, etc? Yeah. Could he have reread the original message and saw I had mentioned a mattress? Yeah. A number of things could have been done to give an accurate estimate and a lot of this is just a failure of an owner to get all the info they needed to give the best customer service experience. I would have been happy to provide any additional info they needed and had I failed to do so, it would have been on me. That’s not the case here. I was told one price; given a discount; given an inflated price when the time of service came and just gave them all the cash I had on me to get he service done...and I’m still stuck with a mattress...but again, at least the guys who came to haul my stuff were great. Hats off to them!

So that’s my experience. It’s disappointing - I’m moving in 6 months and was hoping to use these guys to take an old loveseat and some other old furniture that I planned to dump rather then ship across the country. Now I feel like I should just take a chance with another hauling service and hope for the best. Few things will stop a customer from returning like feeing tricked or taken advantage of and that’s how I feel. Take a chance on this company if you want, just make sure you have some extra $$$ - just because they say it’s going to cost a certain amount, doesn’t mean it will. Also be careful of weather! If it’s raining, just wait for a dry day or risk being rescheduled!</review><UserId.>116309048991713896952<//UserId.>< Resp>
